The bridegroom andthe bride enter theChurch together with the
"Hymn of Joy (Pouro)"and at the end of theservice they exit to the
chant of our Lady theVirgin, "Hail to Mary (<ereMaria)."
During the Pentecost,they chant the hymns ofthe procession of the
Resurrection: "Christ isRisen (<rictoc aǹect/)."
